 1856:     def _m51_canonical_identity(row: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple:
 1857:         """Stable identity for M-51 duplicate detection. Prefers
 1858:         `evidence_id` when present; falls back to normalized

 1860:         evid = row.get("evidence_id")
 1861:         if isinstance(evid, str) and evid:

 1291: 
 1292: def _relevance_floor_selection(
 1293:     *,
 1294:     scored: list[tuple[int, float, str, dict[str, Any]]],
 1295:     relevance_floor: float,
 1296:     full_counts: dict[str, int],
 1297:     primary_trial_anchors: list[str] | None,
 1298: ) -> EvidenceSelection:
 1299:     """I-meta-005 Phase 5 (#989): relevance-floor selection (no max_rows cap).
 1300: 
 1301:     Keep EVERY row whose lexical relevance >= ``relevance_floor``, PLUS any row
 1302:     matching a primary trial anchor (floor-EXEMPT — a relevant primary RCT must
 1303:     never be dropped on a low lexical score). Ranked by ``relevance x authority``
 1304:     (authority = the row's ``authority_score`` sidecar, default 1.0). Each kept
 1305:     row is stamped with the additive ``selection_relevance`` float so
 1306:     ``finding_dedup`` picks representatives on the IDENTICAL score (no recompute
 1307:     drift). Pure; returns SHALLOW COPIES (never mutates the caller's rows).
 1308:     """
 1309:     anchors = list(primary_trial_anchors or [])
 1310: 
 1311:     def _is_anchor(row: dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
 1312:         return any(_m42e_detect_primary_for_anchor(row, a) for a in anchors)
 1313: 
 1314:     def _authority(row: dict[str, Any]) -> float:
 1315:         # Default 1.0 ONLY when authority_score is absent/None — an EXPLICIT 0.0
 1316:         # (genuinely zero-authority row) must rank as 0.0, not be laundered to 1.0
 1317:         # by a falsy `or` (Codex diff-gate P2).
 1318:         a = row.get("authority_score")
 1319:         return 1.0 if a is None else float(a)
 1320: 
 1321:     kept = [
 1322:         item for item in scored
 1323:         if item[1] >= relevance_floor or _is_anchor(item[3])
 1324:     ]
 1325:     kept.sort(
 1326:         key=lambda s: (
 1327:             -(s[1] * _authority(s[3])),
 1328:             _TIER_PRIORITY.get(s[2], 9),
 1329:             s[0],
 1330:         )
 1331:     )
 1332:     selected_rows: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
 1333:     selected_counts: dict[str, int] = {}
 1334:     for idx, score, tier, row in kept:
 1335:         new_row = dict(row)
 1336:         new_row["selection_relevance"] = float(score)
 1337:         selected_rows.append(new_row)
 1338:         selected_counts[tier] = selected_counts.get(tier, 0) + 1
 1339:     anchor_exempt = sum(
 1340:         1 for item in kept
 1341:         if item[1] < relevance_floor and _is_anchor(item[3])
 1342:     )
 1343:     return EvidenceSelection(
 1344:         selected_rows=selected_rows,
 1345:         full_counts=full_counts,
 1346:         selected_counts=selected_counts,
 1347:         dropped_count=len(scored) - len(kept),
 1348:         selection_strategy="relevance_floor_v1",
 1349:         notes=[
 1350:             f"relevance_floor={relevance_floor}: kept {len(kept)}/{len(scored)} "

"""Tests for the #956 source-diversity passes in evidence_selector. NO network / NO spend.

Asserts both passes are SOFT same-tier swaps on post-floor slack: a sub-query origin present in a tier's
pool reaches the selection (round-robin reservation), one domain cannot dominate beyond the soft cap, floors
are never evicted, tier minimums (per-tier counts) are preserved, and the kill-switches restore the prior
non-diverse selection exactly.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import pytest

from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.evidence_selector import (
    _row_domain,
    _row_query_origin,
    select_evidence_for_generation,
)

_Q = "alpha beta gamma delta"


def _row(ev_id, *, tier="T2", origin="A", host="x.com", stmt=_Q):
    return {
        "evidence_id": ev_id,
        "source_url": f"https://{host}/{ev_id}",
        "statement": stmt,
        "direct_quote": stmt,
        "tier": tier,
        "query_origin": origin,
    }


def _off(monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_SELECT_SUBQUERY_RESERVE", "0")
    monkeypatch.setenv("PG_SELECT_DOMAIN_CAP", "0")


def _on(monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.delenv("PG_SELECT_SUBQUERY_RESERVE", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("PG_SELECT_DOMAIN_CAP", raising=False)


def _select(rows, max_rows, anchors=None):
    return select_evidence_for_generation(
        research_question=_Q, protocol=None, classified_sources=[],
        evidence_rows=rows, max_rows=max_rows, primary_trial_anchors=anchors,
    )


# ── helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def test_row_query_origin_and_domain():
    assert _row_query_origin({"query_origin": "X"}) == "X"
    assert _row_query_origin({}) == "_unlabeled"
    assert _row_domain({"source_url": "https://www.fda.gov/drugs"}) == "fda.gov"
    assert _row_domain({}) == ""


# ── sub-query reservation ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
def test_underrepresented_subquery_reaches_selection(monkeypatch):
    _on(monkeypatch)
    # 4 origin-A rows + 1 origin-B row, all T2 same relevance; only 3 slots.
    rows = [_row(f"a{i}", origin="A") for i in range(4)] + [_row("b0", origin="B")]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=3)
    origins = {_row_query_origin(r) for r in sel.selected_rows}
    assert "B" in origins  # the lone sub-topic is not starved


def test_killswitch_off_lets_one_origin_dominate(monkeypatch):
    _off(monkeypatch)
    rows = [_row(f"a{i}", origin="A") for i in range(4)] + [_row("b0", origin="B")]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=3)
    origins = [_row_query_origin(r) for r in sel.selected_rows]
    assert origins == ["A", "A", "A"]  # prior non-diverse behavior (by index)
    assert not any("subquery_reservation" in n for n in sel.notes)


# ── per-domain soft cap ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def test_domain_soft_cap_limits_dominance(monkeypatch):
    _on(monkeypatch)
    # 4 rows on x.com + 2 on y.com, all T2 same origin/relevance; 4 slots, cap=ceil(0.5*4)=2.
    rows = [_row(f"x{i}", host="x.com") for i in range(4)] + [_row(f"y{i}", host="y.com") for i in range(2)]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=4)
    doms = [_row_domain(r) for r in sel.selected_rows]
    assert doms.count("x.com") <= 2  # capped
    assert "y.com" in doms          # under-represented domain pulled in
    assert len(sel.selected_rows) == 4  # no slot left empty


def test_killswitch_off_lets_one_domain_dominate(monkeypatch):
    _off(monkeypatch)
    rows = [_row(f"x{i}", host="x.com") for i in range(4)] + [_row(f"y{i}", host="y.com") for i in range(2)]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=4)
    doms = [_row_domain(r) for r in sel.selected_rows]
    assert doms.count("x.com") == 4  # prior behavior (by index, no cap)
    assert not any("domain_soft_cap" in n for n in sel.notes)


# ── invariants: tier minimums + floors ──────────────────────────────────────
def test_tier_minimums_preserved(monkeypatch):
    # mixed-tier pool: diversity must not change per-tier counts (same-tier swaps).
    rows = (
        [_row(f"t1_{i}", tier="T1", origin="A") for i in range(3)]
        + [_row(f"t2_{i}", tier="T2", origin="A") for i in range(3)]
        + [_row("t2_b", tier="T2", origin="B")]
    )
    _off(monkeypatch)
    base = _select(rows, max_rows=4).selected_counts
    _on(monkeypatch)
    div = _select(rows, max_rows=4).selected_counts
    assert base == div  # per-tier counts identical → no tier dropped below quota


def test_floor_primary_not_evicted_by_diversity(monkeypatch):
    _on(monkeypatch)
    primary = {
        "evidence_id": "surpass2", "tier": "T1",
        "source_url": "https://nejm.org/10.1056/nejmoa2107519",
        "statement": "SURPASS-2 alpha beta gamma delta", "direct_quote": "primary",
        "query_origin": "A",
    }
    # many same-origin/same-domain T1 fillers that the diversity passes would otherwise churn
    fillers = [_row(f"f{i}", tier="T1", origin="A", host="x.com") for i in range(8)]
    sel = _select([*fillers, primary], max_rows=3, anchors=["SURPASS-2"])
    ids = {r["evidence_id"] for r in sel.selected_rows}
    assert "surpass2" in ids  # named-trial primary floor survives diversity


def test_domain_cap_yields_when_no_same_tier_replacement(monkeypatch):
    _on(monkeypatch)
    # all rows same domain + same tier → cap cannot swap (no other-domain same-tier row); must yield, not crash
    rows = [_row(f"x{i}", host="x.com", origin="A") for i in range(6)]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=4)
    assert len(sel.selected_rows) == 4  # full, no empty slot
    assert all(_row_domain(r) == "x.com" for r in sel.selected_rows)  # yielded


def test_short_pool_path_unaffected(monkeypatch):
    _on(monkeypatch)
    # pool <= max_rows → short-pool path keeps everything; diversity is moot there.
    rows = [_row(f"a{i}", origin="A") for i in range(2)] + [_row("b0", origin="B")]
    sel = _select(rows, max_rows=10)
    assert len(sel.selected_rows) == 3  # all kept, no churn

  971: def apply_full_capability_benchmark_slate() -> None:
  972:     """Make the full-capability slate AUTHORITATIVE over .env / conservative defaults (FLOOR semantics).
  973: 
  974:     Codex diff-gate iter-2 P1-1: ``setdefault`` was WRONG. ``load_dotenv`` (openrouter_client import)
  975:     puts .env values into ``os.environ`` BEFORE this slate runs, so a conservative .env default
  976:     (e.g. ``PG_MOST_MAX_EVIDENCE=300``, ``PG_AGENTIC_WEB_PER_ROUND=6``) SURVIVED the setdefault and
  977:     silently throttled the benchmark below the slate. Fix: every numeric key is a **FLOOR** —
  978:     ``max(existing, slate)`` — so a HIGHER operator/.env value (more capability, e.g.
  979:     ``PG_LLM_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=600`` in .env) is KEPT, but a LOWER default is RAISED to full capability.
  980:     No silent downgrade in either direction (operator no-downgrade directive). Feature flags in
  981:     ``_BENCHMARK_FORCE_ON_FLAGS`` are FORCED ON (a benchmark feature off is a capability downgrade).
  982:     Exact-value flags in ``_BENCHMARK_FORCE_EXACT_FLAGS`` are forced to their slate value.
  983: 
  984:     Codex diff-gate iter-2 P1-2: MUST run BEFORE the sweep / live_retriever / state imports, which cache
  985:     ``PG_LIVE_CONTENT_MAX`` / ``PG_LIVE_HTTP_TIMEOUT`` / ``PG_AGENTIC_WEB_PER_ROUND`` as import-time module
  986:     constants. ``main()`` applies it before ``load_locked_questions()``; ``run_gate_b_query`` applies it
  987:     before the sweep import. ``preflight_full_capability`` then validates the LIVE module constants so a
  988:     too-late application is caught fail-closed.
  989:     """
  990:     for name, value in _FULL_CAPABILITY_BENCHMARK_SLATE.items():
  991:         if name in _BENCHMARK_FORCE_ON_FLAGS or name in _BENCHMARK_FORCE_EXACT_FLAGS:
  992:             os.environ[name] = value                       # force exact value — no silent benchmark drift
  993:             continue
  994:         try:
  995:             current = float(os.environ.get(name, value))
  996:         except (TypeError, ValueError):
  997:             current = float(value)
  998:         os.environ[name] = str(int(max(current, float(value))))   # FLOOR: raise-to-slate, keep-if-higher
  999:     # PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN is an import-time constant in openrouter_client (cached before this slate via
 1000:     # the role import chain), so the floor above only fixes the env; sync the live module global too so
 1001:     # check_run_budget enforces the floored cap and run_one_query's manifest reads it (Codex iter-1 P1-2).
 1002:     from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import set_max_cost_per_run
 1003:     set_max_cost_per_run(float(os.environ["PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN"]))

 1006: def preflight_full_capability() -> None:
 1007:     """FAIL CLOSED if the effective benchmark config is below full capability or unobservable — so a
 1008:     silent throttle (the ~40-URL bug) can NEVER reach a paid run undetected. Raises RuntimeError."""
 1009:     for name, floor in _BENCHMARK_PREFLIGHT_FLOORS.items():
